\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01101}01101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01102}01102 \textcolor{comment}{// [From MSDN]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01103}01103 \textcolor{comment}{// If the depth buffer currently bound to the outputmerger stage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01104}01104 \textcolor{comment}{// has a UNORM format or no depth buffer is bound the bias value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01105}01105 \textcolor{comment}{// is calculated like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01106}01106 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01107}01107 \textcolor{comment}{// Bias = (float)DepthBias * r + SlopeScaledDepthBias* MaxDepthSlope;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01108}01108 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01109}01109 \textcolor{comment}{// where r is the minimum representable value > 0 in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01110}01110 \textcolor{comment}{// depth-\/buffer format converted to float32.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01111}01111 \textcolor{comment}{// [/End MSDN]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01112}01112 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01113}01113 \textcolor{comment}{// For a 24-\/bit depth buffer, r = 1 / 2\string^24.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01114}01114 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01115}01115 \textcolor{comment}{// Example: DepthBias = 100000 ==> Actual DepthBias = 100000 / 2 \string^ 24 = .006}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01116}01116 \textcolor{comment}{// These values are highly scene dependent, and you will need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01117}01117 \textcolor{comment}{// to experiment with these values for your scene to find the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01118}01118 \textcolor{comment}{// best values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01119}01119     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01120}01120     \textcolor{comment}{// step4: PSO for shadow map pass.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_shadow_map_app_8cpp_source_l01121}01121     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
